<ul>
<li><a title="Aaron D. O'Connell" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Aaron_D._O%27Connell">Aaron D. O'Connell</a>&nbsp;(born 1981), U.S. &ndash; first&nbsp;<a title="Quantum machine" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Quantum_machine">Quantum machine</a></li>
